\DoxyCodeLine{1987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1988      \textcolor{comment}{// The purpose of the following global constants is to prevent redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989      \textcolor{comment}{// reloading of the constants when they are referenced by more than one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990      \textcolor{comment}{// separate inline math routine called within the same function.  Declaring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991      \textcolor{comment}{// a constant locally within a routine is sufficient to prevent redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992      \textcolor{comment}{// reloads of that constant when that single routine is called multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1993      \textcolor{comment}{// times in a function, but if the constant is used (and declared) in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1994      \textcolor{comment}{// separate math routine it would be reloaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1995 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2237         \textcolor{comment}{// Splat the scalar value (It's really a float)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2238         vScale = \_mm\_set1\_epi32(\textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(uScale));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239         \textcolor{comment}{// Multiply by the reciprocal (Perform a right shift by DivExponent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2240         vResult = \_mm\_mul\_ps(vResult, \_mm\_castsi128\_ps(vScale));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2241         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} vResult;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2242 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2243     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2245     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2246 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2247     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_direct_x_acbabae277338f756c75bce81edf16f75}{XMVECTOR}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_direct_x_math_8h_a9720795adbcd10e5807c888cf625f6fa}{XM\_CALLCONV}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_direct_x_a6e971b8fde88ddb1725a7b88a3f33efc}{XMVectorSplatConstantInt}}(int32\_t IntConstant) \textcolor{keyword}{noexcept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2248     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2249         assert(IntConstant >= -\/16 \&\& IntConstant <= 15);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2250 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_XM\_NO\_INTRINSICS\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2251 }
